msg:1. The environment of Evergrande Five Kingdoms Hot Spring Hotel is great, with birds singing and flowers blooming, green grass and beautiful flowers. For those who like quietness and hot springs, this will be a great choice.
2. The room service is very good. When you check in, there will be a special housekeeper to add your WeChat, and then you can contact the housekeeper through WeChat for any needs, and the reply speed is very fast, the service attitude is also very good, basically responsive.
3. This place is still a distance away from Evergrande Sea Venice Hotel. It takes 3.5km or about 10 minutes to take a taxi or drive there. For breakfast, you can go there to eat buffet, or you can ask the housekeeper to provide door-to-door delivery. There are photos of breakfast delivered to the room in the photos. Overall, the quality is still very good.
4. As for the Five Kingdoms Hot Spring Tickets and Bihai Silver Beach Tickets given when booking a room, it may be due to seasonal reasons. Whether it is the number of tourists taking a hot spring bath or the number of people in the Bihai Silver Beach scenic area, there are very few people. The scenic area is still under renovation, and the sea water looks a bit dirty.
Others:
The air conditioner has been turned on when entering the room, and the room is very warm. Because it happened to be raining in Qidong and it was cold outside, it was still very considerate.
When you enter the hotel and scenic area, all the service staff will smile and wave at you. They are very enthusiastic, which is worth affirming.
In short, the overall stay experience is good, and it is recommended to try!

msg:I checked into the Japanese-style hot spring villa No. 655 on the fourth day of the Chinese New Year. The single-story villa is like a large suite, with 2 bedrooms and 2 living rooms. It is very large, with a separate steam room and SPA room, and an outdoor courtyard. The outdoor private bath is a feature. I asked the housekeeper to help fill the water for 2 nights. It was very artistic to soak in the private bath at night. The large bathtub indoors is just a decoration. The housekeeper said that the water could not be filled in an hour. I tried it and it was true. After 10 minutes, there was no movement, so I gave up and relied on the outdoor one. Because I checked in in the afternoon of the fourth day of the Chinese New Year, there were firecrackers and fireworks outside at night. I, a Shanghainese who had not heard the sound of firecrackers for several years, suddenly remembered that the fifth day of the Chinese New Year was the day to welcome the God of Wealth. I was so excited. I took my son to the courtyard to watch the fireworks in the distance and listen to the sound of firecrackers. I was very excited, but my son didn't seem to be interested and went back to the room in 2 seconds... The children of their generation all had a childhood without fireworks and firecrackers, but it was not surprising that there was no comparison. I asked the housekeeper, and there are fireworks shows on the beach from New Year's Eve to the second day of the New Year. Fortunately, we went to Qi Tang City on the fifth day of the New Year to watch the fireworks show and iron flower, and finally felt the a**osphere of the New Year. The villa is very good and comfortable to live in. The housekeeper is also very considerate, available at any time and responds quickly, especially when we are playing outside and haven't got home yet, the housekeeper has prepared the private bath, so we can soak in it as soon as we get back. It's really great. The welcome fruit and MINI BAR are also very good, with a variety of fruits, and soft drinks and coffee capsules are not stingy at all. It is worth recommending.

name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Thai-Style Duplex Family Friendly Villa
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:6 Reviews
rating:1.2
posted:Posted August 8, 2023
msg:Sure enough, a good review may not necessarily be an expression of true feelings, but a negative review must be an expression of true feelings. I saw some bad reviews before I booked the room. They were very sincere, but I was still lucky and I really deserved it.
The hotel is located in an extremely remote location, with a row of wind power stations in front of the door, making it an inaccessible location. The so-called lobby has only one staff member. The next day, even the lobby was guarded by General Tie.
It is commendable to add the housekeeper's WeChat account and answer all questions, and handle problems in a timely manner. but! If you need to ask the housekeeper for even the most basic hotel services, and then spend time waiting for you to solve it, does it appear that your team is extremely unprofessional, unserious, and irresponsible?
Sanitation is worrying. Returning to the cleaned room, from the first floor to the second floor, there were muddy footprints on the corridor. Is this a hint that someone has been in my room before? Come on, let's analyze it from the footprints. Is this a gentleman or a lady? What did he come in for?
The environment on the beach is also very bad. In the infinity pool, there is a mask floating directly, and all kinds of garbage can be seen on the beach. What is even more disgusting is that I saw several tourists spitting directly on the beach. This is really unbearable. I reported it to the hotel and they replied, "We can't control other guests." I believe this must be their true thoughts, which is why they said it so confidently. At first glance, you are right. How can I take care of other people? But think about it on the other hand, how can a team that adheres to this concept manage this beach carefully? As long as you pay the money and buy the ticket, you can do whatever you want later. As for the dirty and smelly things, leave it to the sea. I believe that the sea has strong self-purification power.
Parking is a big problem. It takes 10 minutes to drive from Gokoku Hot Spring to the main hotel. After arriving at the hotel, find a vacant parking space (difficulty rating: five stars). Then it takes at least 10 minutes to walk to a restaurant or the beach. It is very difficult in the summer. . By the way, there is a shuttle bus service, every 30 minutes, but there is no shuttle bus in the morning on weekdays, so what should I do? Well, you can stay in the room and watch TV...
The quality of breakfast cannot be complimented. There are few varieties, poor quality control, and the ingredients are quite cheap. If you want to find a box of branded yogurt, it is impossible. You will never miss any corner where you can save money. The steaming stall is not even willing to turn on the steam, and the cold Hanamaki It was also the first time I ate it.
As a hotel that focuses on families and children, the performance is surprising. Regardless of whether itâ€™s a hotel or a beach, I visually estimate that 95% of the trips are for families. The groups you serve are all children. Itâ€™s okay to be unprofessional, but your confusing attitude is disgusting.
